of the Council of Europe, which allows to understand its purpose and provide legal assessment of various 
aspects of its activities. On the basis of the analysis of documents adopted –¨—É the Commission , their 
types and content, the author considers peculiarities of interpretation –¨—É the Commission of national 
legal rules. lnterpretation of the national law –¨—É the Commission, which the author categorizes as –∞ kind 
of international interpretation , is carried out through the lens of multifunctional legal standards of the
